		<text>&lt;html&gt;
  &lt;head&gt;
		&lt;style&gt;
			p {padding:0px; margin:0px;}
		&lt;/style&gt;
	&lt;/head&gt;
  &lt;body&gt;
    &lt;p data-pm-slice=&quot;0 0 []&quot;&gt;
Parent Rule and Parent Object Example

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
We have defined two validation rules:

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;quot;&lt;b&gt;Disapproved Requirements&lt;/b&gt;&amp;quot; is a simple validation rule that identifies requirements with a &amp;quot;disapproved&amp;quot; status value.

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;quot;&lt;b&gt;Package with Disapproved Requirements&lt;/b&gt;&amp;quot; is a simple validation rule that identifies packages containing at least one requirement with a &amp;quot;disapproved&amp;quot; status value.

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
The goal is to group these two rules - specifically, the failure of the package element should serve as the parent for requirement failures in &lt;b&gt;Validation Results&lt;/b&gt; panel.

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
This is achieved by setting the &amp;quot;&lt;b&gt;Parent Rule&lt;/b&gt;&amp;quot; and &amp;quot;&lt;b&gt;Parent Object&lt;/b&gt;&amp;quot; properties for &lt;b&gt;Disapproved Requirements&lt;/b&gt; validation rule:

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Parent Rule&lt;/b&gt;: This value refers to the &amp;quot;Package with Disapproved Requirements&amp;quot; validation rule. The purpose of this property is to relate the two validation rules.

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&amp;#160;

    &lt;/p&gt;

    &lt;p&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Parent Object&lt;/b&gt;: This value is an expression that specifies the grouping criterion. In this case, the expression is &amp;quot;Simple Navigation&amp;quot; with &#39;Owner&#39; criterion selected. That means failure requirements from the &amp;quot;Disapproved Requirements&amp;quot; are grouped under failure package if package is the model owner of such requirements.      
&lt;br&gt;

    &lt;/p&gt;

&lt;/body&gt;
&lt;/html&gt;</text>
